Bagging이 병렬로 학습하는 반면, Boosting은 순차적으로 학습</figcaption></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Boosting 기법의 경우, 정확도가 높게 나타납니다. 하지만, 그만큼 <strong>Outlier에 취약하기도 합니다.</strong></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>서로 다른 모델을 결합하여 새로운 모델을 만들어내는 방법도 있습니다. 대표적으로&nbsp;Stacking</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:separator -->\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n<!-- /wp:separator -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>generated quantities: ppc</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>test whether our model can generate extremes that we see in our data: count the fraction of posterior predictive samples where the max, min of simulated data is more extreme than the actual data</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>kth order statistic from a sample of n independent U(0, 1) variables has the Beta(k, n-k + 1) distribution.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2439} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/image-11.png?fit=620%2C266\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-2439\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>covariate: 설명변수</strong></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>In the divorce example, if we knew x j , the divorce rate in state j last year, for j = 1, . . . , 8, but not which index corresponded to which state, then we would certainly be able to distinguish the eight values of y j , but the joint prior distribution p(x j , y j ) would be the same for each state. For states having the same last year divorce rates x j , we could use grouping and assume partial exchangeability or if there are many possible values for x j (as we would assume for divorce rates) we could assume conditional exchangeability and use x j as <strong>covariate</strong> in regression model. - BDA 중</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>1. unit root test&nbsp;</strong></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>unit root test</strong>는&nbsp;시계열 변수가 non-stationary하고 unit root를 가지는지를 검정</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>귀무가설이 unit root(단위근)을 가짐이며, 대안가설은 사용한 검정 종류에 따라 stationarity, trend stationarity or explosive root로 나뉠 수 있다</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>y_t = D_t + z_t + epsilon_t 에서</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>D_t는 deterministic 성분</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>z_t는 stochastic 성분</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>epsilon_t는 stationary error process</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>unit root test는 stochastic 성분이 unit root을 가지는지, 즉 stationary한지를 알아보는 것</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list -->\n<ul><li>adf (augmented Dickey-Fuller test) 주로 이용</li><li>serial correlation test와 밀접한 관련 있지만, 모든 unit root process는 serisl correlation을 가지는 반면 모든 serially correlated 시계열이 unit root를 가지지는 않음</li></ul>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:list {\"ordered\":true} -->\n<ol><li><strong>AR, MA</strong></li></ol>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>AR(p)</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2209} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/2019-05-02-05.26.34.png\" alt=\"스크린샷 2019-05-02 05.26.34.png\" class=\"wp-image-2209\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>MA(q)</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2210} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/2019-05-02-05.46.17.png\" alt=\"스크린샷 2019-05-02 05.46.17.png\" class=\"wp-image-2210\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>2. cointegration test</strong></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>cointegration은 시계열 변수 collection (X_1, X_2, ... , X_k)에 대한 통계적 성질</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>조합이 다음 두 조건을 만족하면 co-integrated되어있다함</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>먼저 계열들은 차수 d로 integrated돼야하며,</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>둘째 이 계열의 선형조합은 d이하의 차수로 차분</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>y_t와 y_(t-1), ... ,y_(t-k)관계를 설명하는 AR(k)는 ACF로</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>y_t와 epsilon_(t-1), ... , epsilon_(t-k)관계 설명하는 MA(k)는 PACF로</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>ARMA(p, q) 결정 시 ACF, PACF를 그려보고 판단</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>3. ACF, PACF</strong></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>ML 모형 만들때 feature들간의 다중공산성(colinearity)은 피해야, 이를 위해 ACF, PACF그림</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>ACF은&nbsp;autocorrelation between an observation and another observation at a prior time step that includes direct and indirect dependence information</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>PACF은 direct relationship between an observation and its lag. This would suggest that there would be no correlation for lag values beyond&nbsp;<em>k로&nbsp;</em>earlier lag에서 explained된 components들은 무시. 즉, only get the lags which have the correlation with the residual i.e the component not explained by earlier lags (이전 lag에서 설명되지 못했던 correlation with the residual만 관찰됨)</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>따라서 AR(p)의 경우 lag=p 이상에서 PACF가 급격히 떨어짐</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>p에서 PACF PLOT이 처음으로 upper confidence interval을 넘음</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2212} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/2019-05-02-05.47.11.png\" alt=\"스크린샷 2019-05-02 05.47.11.png\" class=\"wp-image-2212\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>ACF</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2211} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/2019-05-02-05.47.01.png\" alt=\"스크린샷 2019-05-02 05.47.01.png\" class=\"wp-image-2211\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>PACF</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2213} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/2019-05-02-05.47.01-1.png\" alt=\"스크린샷 2019-05-02 05.47.01.png\" class=\"wp-image-2213\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>4. model selection criteria: AIC, BIC, &nbsp;(WAIC)</strong></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>fit all ARMA(p, q) models with orders p ≤ pmax and q ≤ qmax and choose the values of p and q which minimizes some model selection criteria (AIC, BIC, WAIC 등)</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2208} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/2019-05-02-05.22.10.png\" alt=\"스크린샷 2019-05-02 05.22.10.png\" class=\"wp-image-2208\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>practical Bayesian model evaluation은 leave-one-out cross-validation과 WAIC를 사용함</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2217} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/2019-05-02-06.57.23.png\" alt=\"스크린샷 2019-05-02 06.57.23.png\" class=\"wp-image-2217\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>WAIC</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list -->\n<ul><li>makes no assumption about the shape of the posterior.</li><li>provides an approximation of the <strong>out-of-sample deviance</strong> that converges to the leave-one-out cross-validation approximation in a large sample. But in a finite sample, it can disagree. It can disagree because it has a different target—it isn’t trying to approximate the cross-validation score, but rather guess the out-of-sample K-L Divergence.</li></ul>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>LOOCV도 bayesian에서 많이 사용하는데, 시계열에 적용하기는 어려울듯</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:embed {\"url\":\"http://www.stat.columbia.edu/~gelman/research/published/waic_understand3.pdf\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-embed\"><div class=\"wp-block-embed__wrapper\">\nhttp://www.stat.columbia.edu/~gelman/research/published/waic_understand3.pdf\n</div></figure>\n<!-- /wp:embed -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>5. Granger causality</strong><br>예측에 기반한 통게적 개념<br>신호 x1이 granger-causes 신호 x2하면,<br>x1과거값이 x2예측에 필요한 정보를 포함하고 있어야</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>spurious correlation:</strong></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>연관되어있지만(예: 상관계수 큼) 인과적 연관성은 없을 때</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n<p>repeatedly samples (with replacement) from a data set according to uniform distribution</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>diverse models on different random samples</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>each bootstrap sample is likely to leave out about a third of data instances (1 – 1/n)^n</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2448} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/image-13.png?fit=620%2C234\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-2448\"/><figcaption>Boosting도 Bagging과 동일하게 복원 랜덤 샘플링을 하지만, 가중치를 부여한다는 차이점이 있습니다. Bagging이 병렬로 학습하는 반면, Boosting은 순차적으로 학습</figcaption></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Boosting 기법의 경우, 정확도가 높게 나타납니다. 하지만, 그만큼 <strong>Outlier에 취약하기도 합니다.</strong></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>서로 다른 모델을 결합하여 새로운 모델을 만들어내는 방법도 있습니다. 대표적으로&nbsp;Stacking</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:separator -->\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n<!-- /wp:separator -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>generated quantities: ppc</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>test whether our model can generate extremes that we see in our data: count the fraction of posterior predictive samples where the max, min of simulated data is more extreme than the actual data</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>kth order statistic from a sample of n independent U(0, 1) variables has the Beta(k, n-k + 1) distribution.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2439} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/image-11.png?fit=620%2C266\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-2439\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>covariate: 설명변수</strong></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>In the divorce example, if we knew x j , the divorce rate in state j last year, for j = 1, . . . , 8, but not which index corresponded to which state, then we would certainly be able to distinguish the eight values of y j , but the joint prior distribution p(x j , y j ) would be the same for each state. For states having the same last year divorce rates x j , we could use grouping and assume partial exchangeability or if there are many possible values for x j (as we would assume for divorce rates) we could assume conditional exchangeability and use x j as <strong>covariate</strong> in regression model. - BDA 중</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>1. unit root test&nbsp;</strong></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>unit root test</strong>는&nbsp;시계열 변수가 non-stationary하고 unit root를 가지는지를 검정</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>귀무가설이 unit root(단위근)을 가짐이며, 대안가설은 사용한 검정 종류에 따라 stationarity, trend stationarity or explosive root로 나뉠 수 있다</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>y_t = D_t + z_t + epsilon_t 에서</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>D_t는 deterministic 성분</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>z_t는 stochastic 성분</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>epsilon_t는 stationary error process</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>unit root test는 stochastic 성분이 unit root을 가지는지, 즉 stationary한지를 알아보는 것</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list -->\n<ul><li>adf (augmented Dickey-Fuller test) 주로 이용</li><li>serial correlation test와 밀접한 관련 있지만, 모든 unit root process는 serisl correlation을 가지는 반면 모든 serially correlated 시계열이 unit root를 가지지는 않음</li></ul>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:list {\"ordered\":true} -->\n<ol><li><strong>AR, MA</strong></li></ol>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>AR(p)</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2209} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/2019-05-02-05.26.34.png\" alt=\"스크린샷 2019-05-02 05.26.34.png\" class=\"wp-image-2209\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>MA(q)</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2210} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/2019-05-02-05.46.17.png\" alt=\"스크린샷 2019-05-02 05.46.17.png\" class=\"wp-image-2210\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>2. cointegration test</strong></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>cointegration은 시계열 변수 collection (X_1, X_2, ... , X_k)에 대한 통계적 성질</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>조합이 다음 두 조건을 만족하면 co-integrated되어있다함</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>먼저 계열들은 차수 d로 integrated돼야하며,</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>둘째 이 계열의 선형조합은 d이하의 차수로 차분</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>y_t와 y_(t-1), ... ,y_(t-k)관계를 설명하는 AR(k)는 ACF로</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>y_t와 epsilon_(t-1), ... , epsilon_(t-k)관계 설명하는 MA(k)는 PACF로</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>ARMA(p, q) 결정 시 ACF, PACF를 그려보고 판단</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>3. ACF, PACF</strong></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>ML 모형 만들때 feature들간의 다중공산성(colinearity)은 피해야, 이를 위해 ACF, PACF그림</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>ACF은&nbsp;autocorrelation between an observation and another observation at a prior time step that includes direct and indirect dependence information</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>PACF은 direct relationship between an observation and its lag. This would suggest that there would be no correlation for lag values beyond&nbsp;<em>k로&nbsp;</em>earlier lag에서 explained된 components들은 무시. 즉, only get the lags which have the correlation with the residual i.e the component not explained by earlier lags (이전 lag에서 설명되지 못했던 correlation with the residual만 관찰됨)</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>따라서 AR(p)의 경우 lag=p 이상에서 PACF가 급격히 떨어짐</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>p에서 PACF PLOT이 처음으로 upper confidence interval을 넘음</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2212} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/2019-05-02-05.47.11.png\" alt=\"스크린샷 2019-05-02 05.47.11.png\" class=\"wp-image-2212\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>ACF</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2211} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/2019-05-02-05.47.01.png\" alt=\"스크린샷 2019-05-02 05.47.01.png\" class=\"wp-image-2211\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>PACF</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2213} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/2019-05-02-05.47.01-1.png\" alt=\"스크린샷 2019-05-02 05.47.01.png\" class=\"wp-image-2213\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>4. model selection criteria: AIC, BIC, &nbsp;(WAIC)</strong></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>fit all ARMA(p, q) models with orders p ≤ pmax and q ≤ qmax and choose the values of p and q which minimizes some model selection criteria (AIC, BIC, WAIC 등)</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2208} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/2019-05-02-05.22.10.png\" alt=\"스크린샷 2019-05-02 05.22.10.png\" class=\"wp-image-2208\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>practical Bayesian model evaluation은 leave-one-out cross-validation과 WAIC를 사용함</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":2217} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/2019-05-02-06.57.23.png\" alt=\"스크린샷 2019-05-02 06.57.23.png\" class=\"wp-image-2217\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>WAIC</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list -->\n<ul><li>makes no assumption about the shape of the posterior.</li><li>provides an approximation of the <strong>out-of-sample deviance</strong> that converges to the leave-one-out cross-validation approximation in a large sample. But in a finite sample, it can disagree. It can disagree because it has a different target—it isn’t trying to approximate the cross-validation score, but rather guess the out-of-sample K-L Divergence.</li></ul>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>LOOCV도 bayesian에서 많이 사용하는데, 시계열에 적용하기는 어려울듯</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:embed {\"url\":\"http://www.stat.columbia.edu/~gelman/research/published/waic_understand3.pdf\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-embed\"><div class=\"wp-block-embed__wrapper\">\nhttp://www.stat.columbia.edu/~gelman/research/published/waic_understand3.pdf\n</div></figure>\n<!-- /wp:embed -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>5. Granger causality</strong><br>예측에 기반한 통게적 개념<br>신호 x1이 granger-causes 신호 x2하면,<br>x1과거값이 x2예측에 필요한 정보를 포함하고 있어야</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>spurious correlation:</strong></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>연관되어있지만(예: 상관계수 큼) 인과적 연관성은 없을 때</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph unit별로 다른 사전지식 반영 필요성!\n\n<blockquote>The state space formulation does not admit any new forecasting techniques. Consequently, it does not produce better forecasts than any of the other methods. The state space approach does admit a Bayesian formulation of the problem, in which the model parameters have a prior distribution that represents our degree of belief concerning the values of these coefficients. Then after some history of the process (observation) becomes available, this prior distribution is updated into a posterior distribution. Another formulation allows the coefficients in the regression model to vary through time. - (Wiley Series in Probability and Statistics) Douglas C. Montgomery, Cheryl L. Jennings, Murat Kulahci - Introduction to Time Series Analysis and Forecasting-Wiley (2015)</blockquote>','TUD W4','','draft','open','open','','','','','2019-03-31 04:58:02','2019-03-30 19:58:02','&nbsp;\n\n사전 지식 반영하고, tud에서는 discretization에 사전지식이 반영\n\ntime unit별로 다른 사전지식 반영 필요성!\n<blockquote>The state space formulation does not admit any new forecasting techniques. Consequently, it does not produce better forecasts than any of the other methods. The state space approach does admit a Bayesian formulation of the problem, in which the model parameters have a prior distribution that represents our degree of belief concerning the values of these coefficients. Then after some history of the process (observation) becomes available, this prior distribution is updated into a posterior distribution. Another formulation allows the coefficients in the regression model to vary through time. - (Wiley Series in Probability and Statistics) Douglas C. Montgomery, Cheryl L. My research on Bayes taught me to live by the spirit of gradual updates with simulation-based reliability checks. Below are detailed interests:</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>Strategy for Security and Resilience</strong>: Organizational Regulatory Functions, Preventive Maintenance</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>Generative and Dynamic Model</strong>: System Dynamics Simulation, Hierarchical Bayesian, Generative Adversarial Network</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>Computational Approximators</strong>: Model Checking Diagnostics, Simulation-based Calibration, Monte Carlo Simulation Methods</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":3095,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"http://www.hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/image-3-1024x464.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-3095\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->',975,'https://www.hyunjimoon.com/?p=6805',0,'revision','',0),(3090,1,'2020-11-01 08:28:49','2020-10-31 23:28:49','<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Methodology: simulated-based inference, scalable Bayes, optimization</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Application: reliability prediction, time series</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>1) Simulated-based inference<br>Every inference requires bespoke model and algorithm that considers specific data generating process. However closed form solutions are hard to expect in many cases, more generic solution is required. Simulation-based inference especially on MCMC provides accurate result in reasonable time.<br>I am interested in designing a model and algorithm on this simulation framework. This includes an iterative process of model building and checking. For example, in Bayesian context, adjusting priors and likelihood, analyzing the geometry of posterior space, calibrating and predictive checks are necessary process for a robust inference. I would like to conduct a research on how each steps could be systematized and quantified. Methodologies including simulation based calibration, khat diagnostics, and sensitivity the are my area of interests.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>2) Scalable inference with and for optimization<br>Inference can enhance the system but not directly; based on the inference summaries from different scenarios, they should be compared iteratively with optimization tools, also known as decision theory. One downside of simulation based inference is its expensive cost which could deter this iterative process. Large number of samples that guaranteed inferential accuracy could be a burden which necessitates the need for scalability. This ignited my interest in approximate methods such as variational inference or Laplace approximation. By using measure of discrepancy over a tractable family of approximation distribution, we can optimize our dual need for accuracy and efficiency. I am passionate on designing approximate models with provable guarantees or geometric pathology avoiding algorithms. Not only that, suggesting a better decision with these inferential result is the topic which, I believe, could maximize my contribution to the society.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>3) Reliability Prediction and Time series<br>Ongoing engine failure prediction project with Korean Armed Force have led me to the topic of reliability prediction. Among many forms, I have expertise in time series data. Time series have interpretable components such as trend, seasonality, and event effects. Once these features are properly modeled, it provides both moderately accurate and interpretable results. Moreover, interpretable results of each component could support further decision making process. Additional fascinating property in reliability prediction is its hierarchical structure observed in many equipment system. When hierarchical model is applied to pool information among different subgroups of a system, accuracy and interpretability are greatly advanced. Economical analysis proved that at least a million dollars can be saved based by applying our model to current Korea military system.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":3088,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"http://www.hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/image-935x1024.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-3088\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":3089,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"http://www.hyunjimoon.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/image-1-1024x216.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-3089\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->','Research','','inherit','closed','closed','','975-revision-v1','','','2020-11-01 08:28:49','2020-10-31 23:28:49','<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Methodology: simulated-based inference, scalable Bayes, optimization</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Application: reliability prediction, time series</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>1) Simulated-based inference<br>Every inference requires bespoke model and algorithm that considers specific data generating process. However closed form solutions are hard to expect in many cases, more generic solution is required. Simulation-based inference especially on MCMC provides accurate result in reasonable time.<br>I am interested in designing a model and algorithm on this simulation framework. This includes an iterative process of model building and checking. For example, in Bayesian context, adjusting priors and likelihood, analyzing the geometry of posterior space, calibrating and predictive checks are necessary process for a robust inference. I would like to conduct a research on how each steps could be systematized and quantified. Methodologies including simulation based calibration, khat diagnostics, and sensitivity the are my area of interests.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>2) Scalable inference with and for optimization<br>Inference can enhance the system but not directly; based on the inference summaries from different scenarios, they should be compared iteratively with optimization tools, also known as decision theory. One downside of simulation based inference is its expensive cost which could deter this iterative process. Large number of samples that guaranteed inferential accuracy could be a burden which necessitates the need for scalability. This ignited my interest in approximate methods such as variational inference or Laplace approximation. By using measure of discrepancy over a tractable family of approximation distribution, we can optimize our dual need for accuracy and efficiency. I am passionate on designing approximate models with provable guarantees or geometric pathology avoiding algorithms. Not only that, suggesting a better decision with these inferential result is the topic which, I believe, could maximize my contribution to the society.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>3) Reliability Prediction and Time series<br>Ongoing engine failure prediction project with Korean Armed Force have led me to the topic of reliability prediction.
